GrpcSubscriptionImpl (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc): The adapter class that wraps either a legacy GrpcMuxImpl or NewGrpcMuxImpl. It implements the Subscription interface and provides the bridge between individual subsystems (LDS, CDS, EDS, etc.) and the underlying mux implementation.\\n\\n2. GrpcMuxImpl - SotW (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The legacy State-of-the-World (SotW) gRPC mux implementation. It manages subscriptions to resources over a single gRPC stream using the DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse protocol. It maintains transport-level concerns like stream management, queueing logic, and multiplexing.\\n\\n3. NewGrpcMuxImpl (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The legacy Delta xDS mux implementation. It handles incremental xDS updates using DeltaDiscoveryRequest/DeltaDiscoveryResponse messages, managing resource additions and removals more efficiently than SotW.\\n\\n4. DeltaSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc): The legacy delta protocol state machine that tracks subscription state for the NewGrpcMuxImpl.\\n\\n5. GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory and DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc): Factories that instantiate either GrpcMuxImpl (SotW) or NewGrpcMuxImpl (Delta) based on configuration or runtime flags, providing the selection logic between the two modes.\\n\\nUNIFIED TEMPLATE-BASED COMPONENTS:\\n\\n6. GrpcMuxImpl<S,F,RQ,RS> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The unified generic template that abstracts over subscription state type (S), state factory (F), request type (RQ), and response type (RS). This replaces the need for separate legacy implementations.\\n\\n7. GrpcMuxSotw (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): A concrete specialization of the GrpcMuxImpl template for SotW: GrpcMuxImpl<SotwSubscriptionState, SotwSubscriptionStateFactory, DiscoveryRequest, DiscoveryResponse>. This is the new unified SotW implementation.\\n\\n8. GrpcMuxDelta (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): A concrete specialization of the GrpcMuxImpl template for Delta: GrpcMuxImpl<DeltaSubscriptionState, DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory, DeltaDiscoveryRequest, DeltaDiscoveryResponse>. This is the new unified Delta implementation.\\n\\n9. BaseSubscriptionState<RS,RQ> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h): The abstract base class for protocol state machines, parameterized by response type (RS) and request type (RQ). It handles protocol-agnostic concerns like nonce tracking, error handling, and TTL management.\\n\\n10. SubscriptionStateFactory<T> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h): The abstract factory template for creating SubscriptionState instances.\\n\\n11. SotwSubscriptionStateFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h): Factory implementation for SotwSubscriptionState instances.\\n\\n13. DeltaSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc): Inherits from BaseSubscriptionState<DeltaDiscoveryResponse, DeltaDiscoveryRequest>. Implements the Delta protocol state machine with resource set tracking (added/removed/removed_resources).\\n\\n14. DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h): Factory implementation for DeltaSubscriptionState instances.\\n\\nSUPPORTING COMPONENTS:\\n\\n15. WatchMap (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc): Manages subscriptions from multiple clients (watches) for a given resource type and dispatches updates to each.\\n\\nARCHITECTURE NOTES:\\n\\nThe codebase is currently in a migration phase from the legacy dual-mux system (GrpcMuxImpl and NewGrpcMuxImpl) to the unified template-based system (GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta). The factory in grpc_subscription_factory.cc selects between implementations based on the envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux runtime flag. Both systems coexist to enable gradual migration.\\n\\nThe template design allows both SotW and Delta variants to share transport-level logic (gRPC stream management, queuing, watch management) while specializing for protocol-specific state management. Each SubscriptionState type encapsulates the protocol-specific logic for handling discovery responses, managing subscription interest, and generating requests.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4181,"cache_read_input_tokens":67741,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":4181},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f2166f47-03bc-45f7-b75b-739f994e6de3","uuid":"4c0d1a5c-010a-4cb3-83df-9774daffea9b"}

GrpcMuxImpl<S,F,RQ,RS> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The unified generic template that abstracts over subscription state type (S), state factory (F), request type (RQ), and response type (RS). This replaces the need for separate legacy implementations.\\n\\n7. GrpcMuxSotw (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): A concrete specialization of the GrpcMuxImpl template for SotW: GrpcMuxImpl<SotwSubscriptionState, SotwSubscriptionStateFactory, DiscoveryRequest, DiscoveryResponse>. This is the new unified SotW implementation.\\n\\n8. GrpcMuxDelta (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): A concrete specialization of the GrpcMuxImpl template for Delta: GrpcMuxImpl<DeltaSubscriptionState, DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory, DeltaDiscoveryRequest, DeltaDiscoveryResponse>. This is the new unified Delta implementation.\\n\\n9. BaseSubscriptionState<RS,RQ> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h): The abstract base class for protocol state machines, parameterized by response type (RS) and request type (RQ). It handles protocol-agnostic concerns like nonce tracking, error handling, and TTL management.\\n\\n10. SubscriptionStateFactory<T> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h): The abstract factory template for creating SubscriptionState instances.\\n\\n11. SotwSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc): Inherits from BaseSubscriptionState<DiscoveryResponse, DiscoveryRequest>. Implements the SotW protocol state machine with full state tracking and update generation logic.\\n\\n12. SotwSubscriptionStateFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h): Factory implementation for SotwSubscriptionState instances.\\n\\n13. DeltaSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc): Inherits from BaseSubscriptionState<DeltaDiscoveryResponse, DeltaDiscoveryRequest>. Implements the Delta protocol state machine with resource set tracking (added/removed/removed_resources).\\n\\n14. DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h): Factory implementation for DeltaSubscriptionState instances.\\n\\nSUPPORTING COMPONENTS:\\n\\n15. WatchMap (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc): Manages subscriptions from multiple clients (watches) for a given resource type and dispatches updates to each.\\n\\nARCHITECTURE NOTES:\\n\\nThe codebase is currently in a migration phase from the legacy dual-mux system (GrpcMuxImpl and NewGrpcMuxImpl) to the unified template-based system (GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta). The factory in grpc_subscription_factory.cc selects between implementations based on the envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux runtime flag. Both systems coexist to enable gradual migration.\\n\\nThe template design allows both SotW and Delta variants to share transport-level logic (gRPC stream management, queuing, watch management) while specializing for protocol-specific state management. Each SubscriptionState type encapsulates the protocol-specific logic for handling discovery responses, managing subscription interest, and generating requests.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

protocol implementation in Envoy is organized across two distinct architectures: a legacy dual-mux system and a unified template-based system.\\n\\nLEGACY COMPONENTS:\\n\\n1. GrpcSubscriptionImpl (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc): The adapter class that wraps either a legacy GrpcMuxImpl or NewGrpcMuxImpl. It implements the Subscription interface and provides the bridge between individual subsystems (LDS, CDS, EDS, etc.) and the underlying mux implementation.\\n\\n2. GrpcMuxImpl - SotW (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The legacy State-of-the-World (SotW) gRPC mux implementation. It manages subscriptions to resources over a single gRPC stream using the DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse protocol. It maintains transport-level concerns like stream management, queueing logic, and multiplexing.\\n\\n3. NewGrpcMuxImpl (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The legacy Delta xDS mux implementation. It handles incremental xDS updates using DeltaDiscoveryRequest/DeltaDiscoveryResponse messages, managing resource additions and removals more efficiently than SotW.\\n\\n4. DeltaSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc): The legacy delta protocol state machine that tracks subscription state for the NewGrpcMuxImpl.\\n\\n5. GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory and DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc): Factories that instantiate either GrpcMuxImpl (SotW) or NewGrpcMuxImpl (Delta) based on configuration or runtime flags, providing the selection logic between the two modes.\\n\\nUNIFIED TEMPLATE-BASED COMPONENTS:\\n\\n6. GrpcMuxImpl<S,F,RQ,RS> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The unified generic template that abstracts over subscription state type (S), state factory (F), request type (RQ), and response type (RS). This replaces the need for separate legacy implementations.\\n\\n7. GrpcMuxSotw (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): A concrete specialization of the GrpcMuxImpl template for SotW: GrpcMuxImpl<SotwSubscriptionState, SotwSubscriptionStateFactory, DiscoveryRequest, DiscoveryResponse>. This is the new unified SotW implementation.\\n\\n8. GrpcMuxDelta (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): A concrete specialization of the GrpcMuxImpl template for Delta: GrpcMuxImpl<DeltaSubscriptionState, DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory, DeltaDiscoveryRequest, DeltaDiscoveryResponse>. This is the new unified Delta implementation.\\n\\n9. BaseSubscriptionState<RS,RQ> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h): The abstract base class for protocol state machines, parameterized by response type (RS) and request type (RQ). It handles protocol-agnostic concerns like nonce tracking, error handling, and TTL management.\\n\\n10. SubscriptionStateFactory<T> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h): The abstract factory template for creating SubscriptionState instances.\\n\\n11. SotwSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc): Inherits from BaseSubscriptionState<DiscoveryResponse, DiscoveryRequest>. Implements the SotW protocol state machine with full state tracking and update generation logic.\\n\\n12. SotwSubscriptionStateFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h): Factory implementation for SotwSubscriptionState instances.\\n\\n13. DeltaSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc): Inherits from BaseSubscriptionState<DeltaDiscoveryResponse, DeltaDiscoveryRequest>. DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h): Factory implementation for DeltaSubscriptionState instances.\\n\\nSUPPORTING COMPONENTS:\\n\\n15. WatchMap (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc): Manages subscriptions from multiple clients (watches) for a given resource type and dispatches updates to each.\\n\\nARCHITECTURE NOTES:\\n\\nThe codebase is currently in a migration phase from the legacy dual-mux system (GrpcMuxImpl and NewGrpcMuxImpl) to the unified template-based system (GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta). The factory in grpc_subscription_factory.cc selects between implementations based on the envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux runtime flag. Both systems coexist to enable gradual migration.\\n\\nThe template design allows both SotW and Delta variants to share transport-level logic (gRPC stream management, queuing, watch management) while specializing for protocol-specific state management. Envoy is organized across two distinct architectures: a legacy dual-mux system and a unified template-based system.\\n\\nLEGACY COMPONENTS:\\n\\n1. GrpcSubscriptionImpl (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc): The adapter class that wraps either a legacy GrpcMuxImpl or NewGrpcMuxImpl. It implements the Subscription interface and provides the bridge between individual subsystems (LDS, CDS, EDS, etc.) and the underlying mux implementation.\\n\\n2. GrpcMuxImpl - SotW (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The legacy State-of-the-World (SotW) gRPC mux implementation. It manages subscriptions to resources over a single gRPC stream using the DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse protocol. It maintains transport-level concerns like stream management, queueing logic, and multiplexing.\\n\\n3. NewGrpcMuxImpl (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The legacy Delta xDS mux implementation. It handles incremental xDS updates using DeltaDiscoveryRequest/DeltaDiscoveryResponse messages, managing resource additions and removals more efficiently than SotW.\\n\\n4. DeltaSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc): The legacy delta protocol state machine that tracks subscription state for the NewGrpcMuxImpl.\\n\\n5. GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory and DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc): Factories that instantiate either GrpcMuxImpl (SotW) or NewGrpcMuxImpl (Delta) based on configuration or runtime flags, providing the selection logic between the two modes.\\n\\nUNIFIED TEMPLATE-BASED COMPONENTS:\\n\\n6. GrpcMuxImpl<S,F,RQ,RS> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): The unified generic template that abstracts over subscription state type (S), state factory (F), request type (RQ), and response type (RS). This replaces the need for separate legacy implementations.\\n\\n7. GrpcMuxSotw (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): A concrete specialization of the GrpcMuxImpl template for SotW: GrpcMuxImpl<SotwSubscriptionState, SotwSubscriptionStateFactory, DiscoveryRequest, DiscoveryResponse>. This is the new unified SotW implementation.\\n\\n8. GrpcMuxDelta (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc): A concrete specialization of the GrpcMuxImpl template for Delta: GrpcMuxImpl<DeltaSubscriptionState, DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory, DeltaDiscoveryRequest, DeltaDiscoveryResponse>. This is the new unified Delta implementation.\\n\\n9. BaseSubscriptionState<RS,RQ> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h): The abstract base class for protocol state machines, parameterized by response type (RS) and request type (RQ). It handles protocol-agnostic concerns like nonce tracking, error handling, and TTL management.\\n\\n10. SubscriptionStateFactory<T> template (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h): The abstract factory template for creating SubscriptionState instances.\\n\\n11. SotwSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc): Inherits from BaseSubscriptionState<DiscoveryResponse, DiscoveryRequest>. Implements the SotW protocol state machine with full state tracking and update generation logic.\\n\\n12. SotwSubscriptionStateFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h): Factory implementation for SotwSubscriptionState instances.\\n\\n13. DeltaSubscriptionState (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc): Inherits from BaseSubscriptionState<DeltaDiscoveryResponse, DeltaDiscoveryRequest>. Implements the Delta protocol state machine with resource set tracking (added/removed/removed_resources).\\n\\n14. DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h): Factory implementation for DeltaSubscriptionState instances.\\n\\nSUPPORTING COMPONENTS:\\n\\n15. WatchMap (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc): Manages subscriptions from multiple clients (watches) for a given resource type and dispatches updates to each.\\n\\nARCHITECTURE NOTES:\\n\\nThe codebase is currently in a migration phase from the legacy dual-mux system (GrpcMuxImpl and NewGrpcMuxImpl) to the unified template-based system (GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta). The factory in grpc_subscription_factory.cc selects between implementations based on the envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux runtime flag. Both systems coexist to enable gradual migration.\\n\\nThe template design allows both SotW and Delta variants to share transport-level logic (gRPC stream management, queuing, watch management) while specializing for protocol-specific state management. Each SubscriptionState type encapsulates the protocol-specific logic for handling discovery responses, managing subscription interest, and generating requests.\"\n}\n","numLines":41,"startLine":1,"totalLines":41}}}
